# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```

# CI/CD Integration for Terraform

## Objective
Automate Terraform plans and applies in a secure manner.

## Recommendations
- Use `terraform fmt` and `validate` in pipelines.
- Require manual approval for `terraform apply`.
- Use remote state locking with workspaces.

## Example
```hcl
terraform {
  backend "s3" {
    bucket = "my-terraform-state"
    key    = "state.tfstate"
    region = "us-east-1"
  }
}
```
